  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_7950169b-dc9e-4427-8455-7e1995e6efd5'

<span id="freeTextContainer10512910955147707185">After the disastrous fallout on Halloween and the tragic events that followed in the Hazel Cove Cemetery, Alexandria is left picking up the pieces of her broken life.   <span id="freeText10512910955147707185" style="display:none">After the disastrous fallout on Halloween and the tragic events that followed in the Hazel Cove Cemetery, Alexandria is left picking up the pieces of her broken life. Peter is adjusting. James hates her. Grandma Claudia is gone. Emma is incoherent. Victor went rogue. And Gamma still wants her dead.<br /><br />If that wasn't enough to deal with, two burning questions are driving Alex insane. Who committed that horrible murder in Salem? And what really happened to Ethan?<br /><br />Alex has come to terms with her new life, but she's yet to truly understand the ramifications of being a pureblooded witch in the supernatural world. And now there is a new danger on the horizon. Alex must find a way to fight. To survive. To protect her remaining family members and her closest friends from an unthinkable new enemy. One much more powerful and much more horrifying than the Gamma witch hunting fraternity.</span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/471493597" />
    <a title="Vee" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/15237792-vee"><img alt="Vee" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1566437417p2/15237792.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/471493597?book_show_action=true">Dec 06, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Vee" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Vee" href="/user/show/15237792-vee">Vee</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer471493597" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13519107998902503660">I could not put this series down!!! I was literally at the gym when I finished the second one and I sat there on the treadmill buying the 3rd so I could start it while I finished my workout.<br/><br/>By the end of each book you can't help but to have to read the next to find out what is going to happen. I am impatiently awaiting the 4th installment. It took me 2 weeks to weeks to read all 3.<br/><br/>You love the main character's. Alex is Strong and even though she has so much to deal with she still keeps going and</span>
  <span id="freeText13519107998902503660" style="display:none">I could not put this series down!!! I was literally at the gym when I finished the second one and I sat there on the treadmill buying the 3rd so I could start it while I finished my workout.<br /><br />By the end of each book you can't help but to have to read the next to find out what is going to happen. I am impatiently awaiting the 4th installment. It took me 2 weeks to weeks to read all 3.<br /><br />You love the main character's. Alex is Strong and even though she has so much to deal with she still keeps going and fighting doing what she has to to protect her family and friends. Peter, her best friend turned boyfriend, is just the right mix of stability,protectiveness, and is sweet and caring. In a way he grounds her. While James is a bit more dangerous, very protective, and is constantly butting heads with Peter to win Alex's affections. She has 2 great guys at her side and another to follow and I can't wait to see how this series ends. With each new character introduced into each book you fall more in love with them. Each charater is brought in perfectly and at the right times and just makes everything more complete and entertaining. </span>
  <a data-text-id="13519107998902503660" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/320453645?book_show_action=true">Apr 28, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer320453645" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12571133042616742115">Great read! Highly recommend this new series to all. I honestly think it blows away some of the more popular series out there (you know who you are) – there is enough suspense to keep you flipping to the next page, got it late late Saturday night, and read the whole book on Sunday. <br/><br/>I like the way Bellingeri writes her chapters, where you are left on a mini-cliff hanger at the end of some of them, well done. The characters grow more in this book and I still love the Alex and Peter match and am ge</span>
  <span id="freeText12571133042616742115" style="display:none">Great read! Highly recommend this new series to all. I honestly think it blows away some of the more popular series out there (you know who you are) – there is enough suspense to keep you flipping to the next page, got it late late Saturday night, and read the whole book on Sunday. <br /><br />I like the way Bellingeri writes her chapters, where you are left on a mini-cliff hanger at the end of some of them, well done. The characters grow more in this book and I still love the Alex and Peter match and am getting pretty comfortable with how James fits into the pictures, as long as Bellingeri doesn’t pull the usual “love triangle” card in the next book. It’s good to see young adult characters that are not whinny, or have something to prove or think they can save the word. I like the way Peter was still there at the end but he was trying to figure it all out – I mean come on you would too if….it happened to you…. <br /><br />I refuse to put spoilers in my reviews so they will always be short ones. I think each book should be left up to the reader to discover and to judge instead of making your decision based on a review, but I still want to write a good one that will help you make a decision.<br /><br />I think every character really added to the story line, not one was a “fill in” (or as some of the other reviewers mention in their reviews “a Star Trek Red Shirt Character”), they each played their part well. <br /><br />Looking forward to book 3! <br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="12571133042616742115" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('Q1oSE2gcxsXVsDb5j2s1si7EY90Xu1QBRP2iPKvGROyk9byZMvVYmyh3jwlBY7EmwvzwwhG2VDpvoMW+o4q4bA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('pGCuoVo+9Ot1OOduyGg3s81lvya50XuNntFKT+KSHNhDzwArANdqtYj/Xp4GYLMnIV0sOb/ce7a1jC3N6t7gWA==')})
  }

The Salem Witch Trials of 1692 were an embarrassing stain on America’s revered past. Innocent people were persecuted at the hands of a few overzealous Puritans, but what if real witches existed during those colonial hunts? What if there are witches in present day New England? That’s what Alexandria Ramsey’s crazy grandmother believes. Grandma Claudia claims Alex descends from a long line of New England witches. \n\nModern day witches in Hazel Cove, Massachusetts? Unlikely, but strange things are occurring in the weeks preceding Alex’s seventeenth birthday. Alex is haunted by bizarre recurring nightmares of a man chasing her through the Hazel Cove Cemetery. On a few occasions, when her emotions have spiraled out of control, inanimate objects have shattered around her. But that’s just a coincidence, right? Alex isn’t so sure, especially after a local girl, who supposedly dabbled in witchcraft, was killed in the nearby forest. \n\nAlex knows something strange is happening. With the arrival of a new boy in town, James Van Curen, who is causing problems between Alex and her best friend, Peter, Alex feels like her entire world is on the verge of chaos.
